# 요안-2 원문 로그

**Gamemaster:** 여러분은 지난 밤 요안이 보내온 침투요원들을 저지하는데 성공했습니다.
그들의 계획에 따르면 동이 트기 전까지 텔레포테이션 스크롤로 요새 내부로 병력을 불러올 심
산이었죠.
일행은 침투요원들로부터 입은 상처를 추스르고 다시 모였습니다.
이번에는 정찰에 나갔던 라비니아와 카이젤린도 포함해서 꽤 많이 모였군요.

**라비니아:** (무시무시하다

**Gamemaster:** 일행의 가운데에는 텔레포테이션 서클 스크롤이 존재합니다
이걸 어떻게 쓸지 정해야겠군요.

**럭키:** "좋아. 이쪽도 마법사들이 꽤 갖춰줬으니."
"이제 비등하게 싸울 수 있겠어."

**아르시안 엘다인:** "설마 어제처럼 정말로 그가 있는 곳으로 돌격 할 셈입니까?"

**럭키:** "당근 빳따 아니겠어?"

**라비니아:** "에?"
"돌격?"

**아르시안 엘다인:** "빳…무슨 단어인지는 모르겠지만 일단 하겠다는 의사로 보이는군요"

**시엘라:** Yorumei Rie
"…아직 잠이 덜 깬건가?"

**럭키:** "이 스크롤로 길을 연다. 돌격한다. 요안을 잡는다."
"승리!"

**아르시안 엘다인:** "승리는 무슨! 거기가 어디인줄 알고 가는겁니까!"
"오리진에서 먼 곳이라도 가버리면 저흰 가리아 막지도 못한단말입니다!"

**럭키:** "참 나. 되게 까다롭네."

**침투요원:** "아얏!"

**럭키:** "야! 내 작전 어떻게 생각하냐."
"이 정도면 거의 필승 아니냐?"

**침투요원:** "잘 되면 좋겠지만 말야…"
"요안의 병력은 소수정예라고? 괜찮겠어?"

**럭키:** "우리도 소수 정예인데?"

**침투요원:** "흐음… 너희 개개인의 무력을 직접 본건 아니지만 너희도 꽤 한다는건 인정할게."

**럭키:** "그리고 너희들도 나름 그 소수정예 범주에 속하는 애들 아니었어?"

**침투요원:** "그건 그렇네."

**아르시안 엘다인:** "…"

**럭키:** "거봐. 해볼만하다니까."

**침투요원:** "하지만 요안 본인과 딱 달라붙어 다니는 드래곤본은 차원이 달라."

**피에스타:** (도바킨!)

**아르시안 엘다인:** "드래곤본…?"

**럭키:** "어엉? 드래곤본? 흠… 걔들 중에 뛰어난 싸움꾼이 많긴 하지."
"우리 수비대에도 있어."

**침투요원:** "응. 애지중지 끼고 다니던걸?"

**라비니아:** "드래곤본들은 무시무시한 불꽃을 토해냅니다요"

**침투요원:** "보통 사이가 아닐거라고."

**아르시안 엘다인:** "…즉, 그 드래곤본을 우선으로 제압 한다면 항복의 가능성도 있다는 얘기입니까?"

**럭키:** "자. 마법사들. 너희들 차례야. 불에 대한 대응은."
"당연히 준비해뒀겠지?"

**침투요원:** "요안 본인이 소중하게 여기는거 같으니까."

**라비니아:** "없습니다요"

**럭키:** "요안이 화염 주문을 쓴다는 정보는 이미 진작에 있었는데. 아무 대비도 안했다면."

**침투요원:** "잘 협박하면 될지도?"

**럭키:** "너희는 깡통 마법사야."

**아르시안 엘다인:** "제 종족이야 당신이 잘 아실테니…화염에 저항이 있습니다"

**피에스타:** "하하- 그런건 제겐 필요 없어요-"

**라비니아:** "럭키상병님은 강력한 주먹에 대한 대비를 했습니까요?"

**럭키:** "내 주먹인데 왜 대비하냐! 멍청아."

**아르시안 엘다인:** @요원의 말을 듣고는 "협박이라…상황에 따라 고려를 해봐야겠군요"

**라비니아:** "비슷합니다요"

**피에스타:** "그래서, 정말 우리가 반대로 그들에게 쳐들어가려고요?"

**럭키:** "그럼 걔들이 오는 것만 받아치게? 그래서 어느세월에 해결해."

**피에스타:** "그럼 하려면 빨리 하는게 낫지 않겠어요? 기다리고 있으면, 텔레포테이션 서클이 설치되지 않
는것에 의문을 품고 대비할거라고요?"

**병졸:** "확실히 이미 동이 튼지 꽤 시간이 지났죠."

**럭키:** "그치. 빨리 하자."
"야 마법사들. 일해."

**아르시안 엘다인:** "…하아."

**라비니아:** "히에엑…"

**시엘라:** Yorumei Rie
"마법사들을 적 진영 한가운데에 집어넣는건 별로 좋은 생각이 아닌거같다만…"

**아르시안 엘다인:** "수비대도 아닌데 일 하라고 명령을 받는 마법사라니. 제 처우에 대해 다시 생각해야 할게 많군
요"
"우선, 모이시길"

**럭키:** "잠깐만."

**라비니아:** (그리고 마법사가 있다면 마법책에 필사를 한다)

**피에스타:** "설치할 장소를 잡아두고, 소환하는게 좋겠어요."

**럭키:** 잠시 머리를 쓰는 시늉을 합니다

**라비니아:** "?"

**럭키:** "혹시 변장 주문 가진 사람?"

**아르시안 엘다인:** "…변장이면 그 흰머리 사제가 잘했습니다만?"

**카이젤린:** 밀메0
@꾸벅꾸벅

**럭키:** "아무도 없어?" 노골적으로 실망한 표정

**병졸:** 발레리우스는 아직 돌아오지 않았군요

**라비니아:** "라비니아는동물로 변신할수는 있습니다요"

**럭키:** "너희들 잘하는게 대체 뭐야."

**시엘라:** Yorumei Rie
(생각해보니 변장도구를 안샀구나

**아르시안 엘다인:** "그런 당신은 주먹질 말고 잘하는게 뭡니까…!"

**럭키:** "잘생겼잖아."

**라비니아:** "에?"

**피에스타:** "확률이 없진 않은데, 해드려요? 자수정아카데미 비전의 주문이 있는데."

**럭키:** "하아… 어쩔 수 없지. 저기 딱 포로도 있는데."
"똑같이 분장해서 한 명이 들어가면."
"반대편 상황도 볼 수 있고 감쪽같잖아."

**피에스타:** "흐음. 텔레포테이션 서클은요. 차원문이 아니라고요?"

**아르시안 엘다인:** "…그 다음은 그 사제처럼 적진에서 이리저리 숨어서 눈치 보는겁니까? 그런거라면 더 위험하
다고 생각합니다만"

**럭키:** "그래에?"
"몰라! 똑같은거 아냐?"

**시엘라:** Yorumei Rie
"반대로 우리가 저 녀석들의 옷을 덮어쓰는건 어떤가?"

**라비니아:** "그런데 한가지 궁금한게"

**피에스타:** "특정한 서클로 이동하려면, 그 서클의 주문 구결을 알아야해요. 상대쪽으로 가려면, 이 감자통
에 있는 분이 알려줘야겠죠."

**라비니아:** "쓰러트린 적들의 옷을 뺏어서 들어가면 되는거 아닙니까요?"

**침투요원:** "마법사 아가씨가 잘 아네. 수비대원 오빠는 좀 새겨들을 필요가 있겠어."

**라비니아:** "문제가 되는건 도착하자마자 기습했을때 아닙니까요?"

**럭키:** 감자통을 발로 찹니다

**아르시안 엘다인:** "…"

**피에스타:** "이 스크롤에 적혀있는건, 이 서클의 주소도 구결이 적혀있으니 이미 알고 있는 상대방은 이 곳
으로 텔레포트하는게 가능하지만, 우리는 아니라는거죠."

**라비니아:** "난폭합니다요…"

**럭키:** "너 잘 생각해. 재판 가면 너한테 유리한 증언 해줄 것은 저 여자가 아니라 나야."

**아르시안 엘다인:** "그럼 이 경우에는 차라리 그 요안이 여기로 오게 하는게 더 나을지도 모른다는 것이군요"

**침투요원:** "으윽… 알겠다고. 이쪽에서 넘어가는 방법도 알고 있긴 하다고."

**럭키:** "오-?"

**침투요원:** "날 도망치게 해주면 적극적으로 협조할게~"

**럭키:** "흠… 여기서 사법 거래라~"

**침투요원:** "어차피 나는 뒷조직 출신이라서 말야. 돌아가면 죄가 꽤 무거워질거거든."
"그러니까 죄의 경감은 딱히 못바란다는 거지."

**럭키:** "에엥… 여죄가 꽤 화려한가 보네."

**침투요원:** "암살자로 먹고 살려면 어쩔 수 없지?"

**아르시안 엘다인:** "…이미 저 여자 외의 자들은 죽은 것 같지만 어떡하시겠습니까?"

**럭키:** "음!" 하늘을 쳐다보며 눈을 감습니다. "흉악범을 풀어주는건 내 스타일이 아닌데."
"오리진 시민들의 운명에 경각에 달했으니 어쩔 수 없나."
"하지만 풀어주는건 나중이야. 일단 네가 말한게 사실인지는 확인해야지."
"효과가 있으면 일 끝나고 풀어줄게."

**침투요원:** "뭐? 그럼 너희가 실패하면?"

**럭키:** "우리가 실패하면 요안이 널 풀어주겠지. 무슨 걱정이야."

**침투요원:** "내가 분걸 모를리가!"

**럭키:** "어… 그것도 그런가?"

**라비니아:** "어쩐지 럭키상병님은 경비대가 되지 않고 잘못 자랐으면"
"전형적으로 자기의 행복이 모두의 행복이라고 생각하는 사람의 전형이 될거라고 생각합니다
요"

**아르시안 엘다인:** "…"

**시엘라:** Yorumei Rie
"자기소개는 나중에 해도 된다고 본다만."

**럭키:** 그럼 대거 하나를 꺼내서 침투요원 눈 앞에 던져놓습니다. "좋아. 우리가 마법으로 그쪽으로 넘
어가면 이 단검으로 알아서 풀고 도망가."

**라비니아:** "히에에?"

**침투요원:** "좋아. 거래 성립인가?"

**피에스타:** "….왜 쪼는거에요?"
"침투요원이 7명이나 되는데."

**럭키:** "그래. 하지만 다음에 또 나한테 체포되면 알짤 없어."

**피에스타:** "감자통 요원이 아니라 다른사람에게 얻었다고 둘러대면되죠."
"죽은 자는 말이 없는걸요."

**침투요원:** "살아있는건 나뿐이잖아? 그 아가씨 성격에 거슬리는건 냅둘리가 없거든."

**피에스타:** "그럼 계속 살고 싶으면, 우리에게 붙어서 싸우는건 어때요?"
"어차피 도망치면 살 수 있나? 그 말대로라면 어차피 죽을텐데."

**시엘라:** Yorumei Rie
"일단 그 거래 내용은 문제가 많군. 거짓말로 엉뚱한 곳에 보내도 우리가 돌아오는 길을 모르니
멋대로 도망칠 수 있는 거 아닌가?"

**침투요원:** "아… 원래 고용주한테 덤비라고? 보는 눈이 하나라도 남으면 좀 곤란한데."

**피에스타:** "우리가 이기면, 당신이 뭐 잘 살아가겠어요? 결국 쿠데타 가담자인건 변함 없는데. 이제라도 다
른쪽에 붙어서 처벌이라도 적게 받아야죠."
"동앗줄, 제대로 갈아타는게 좋아보이네요."

**아르시안 엘다인:** "동앗줄이라…"

**Gamemaster:** 설득 Check

"좋아. 너희가 텔레포트 하는데에 같이 타줄게."

**피에스타:** Metamagic: Extended Spell
Cost: 1 Sorcery Point
When you cast a spell that has a duration of 1 minute or longer, you can spend
1 Sorcery Point to double its duration to a maximum duration of 24 hours.
If the affected spell requires Concentration, you have Advantage on any saving
throw you make to maintain that Concentration.

**럭키:** "죽기 전에 착한 일 한 번 하면 좋잖아."

**피에스타:** Sense Lifeblood
As part of casting this spell, you must expend two Hit Point Dice or the spell
automatically fails. The lifeblood flowing within creatures tells you its secrets.
Creatures that have Immunity to the Exhaustion condition are immune to this
spell. Until the spell ends, you can determine if creatures you can see are
related biologically. In addition, you know if a creature’s Hit Points are at
maximum, below maximum, at half, or below half. Once on each of your turns
when you hit a Bloodied creature with an attack roll using a weapon, Unarmed
Strike, or spell, you can cause the target to take extra Necrotic damage. To
determine this damage, roll the Hit Point Dice expended to cast the spell.
Using a Higher-Level Spell Slot. Your Concentration can last longer with a spell
slot of level 3-4 (up to 1 hour) or 5+ (up to 8 hours).

**피에스타:** Blood Bolt
You hurl a twisting bolt of blood at a creature within range. Make a ranged spell
attack against the target. On a hit, the target takes 1d6 Necrotic damage, and
you gain a number of Temporary Hit Points equal to your Proficiency Bonus.
Cantrip Upgrade. The damage increases by 1d6 when you reach levels 5 (2d6),
11 (3d6), and 17 (4d6).
🎲 1d20 + 5 + 2 = 9

**아르시안 엘다인:** Restore Balance
Your connection to the plane of absolute order allows you to equalize chaotic
moments. When a creature you can see within 60 feet of yourself is about to roll
a d20 with Advantage or Disadvantage, you can take a Reaction to prevent the
roll from being affected by Advantage and Disadvantage.
You can use this feature a number of times equal to your Charisma modifier
(minimum of once), and you regain all expended uses when you finish a Long
Rest.

**Gamemaster:** 럭키 heals 8 HP

**럭키:** Deflect Attacks
When an attack roll hits you and its damage includes Bludgeoning, Piercing, or
Slashing damage, you can take a Reaction to reduce the attack’s total damage
against you. The reduction equals 1d10 plus your Dexterity modifier and Monk
level.
If you reduce the damage to 0, you can expend 1 Focus Point to redirect some
of the attack’s force. If you do so, choose a creature you can see within 5 feet of
yourself if the attack was a melee attack or a creature you can see within 60 feet
of yourself that isn’t behind Total Cover if the attack was a ranged attack. That
creature must succeed on a Dexterity saving throw or take damage equal to two
rolls of your Martial Arts die plus your Dexterity modifier. The damage is the
same type dealt by the attack.
🎲 1d10 + 5 + 5 = 16

**시엘라:** Yorumei Rie

**럭키:** Deflect Attacks
When an attack roll hits you and its damage includes Bludgeoning, Piercing, or
Slashing damage, you can take a Reaction to reduce the attack’s total damage
against you. The reduction equals 1d10 plus your Dexterity modifier and Monk
level.
If you reduce the damage to 0, you can expend 1 Focus Point to redirect some
of the attack’s force. If you do so, choose a creature you can see within 5 feet of
yourself if the attack was a melee attack or a creature you can see within 60 feet
of yourself that isn’t behind Total Cover if the attack was a ranged attack. That
creature must succeed on a Dexterity saving throw or take damage equal to two
rolls of your Martial Arts die plus your Dexterity modifier. The damage is the
same type dealt by the attack.

**요안의 마법병:** 분쇄
사거리 내에서 당신이 지정한 지점에 엄청난 굉음이 터지며 울려퍼집니다. 해당 지점 반경
10ft 이내의 모든 크리처는 건강 내성 굴림을 굴려야 하며, 실패할 시 3d8점의 천둥 피해를
입게 됩니다. 내성에 성공한 경우 피해는 절반으로 줄어듭니다. 만약 바위나 수정, 혹은 금속
등으로 만들어진 크리처가 주문에 영향을 받았을 경우, 해당 크리처는 내성 굴림에 불리함을
받게 됩니다.
주문의 범위 내에 다른 누군가가 장비하거나 들고 있지 않은 비마법적 물체가 있다면, 해당
물체 역시 피해를 받게 됩니다.
상위시전. 당신이 3레벨 이상의 주문 슬롯을 사용하여 이 주문을 시전할 경우, 상승한 주문
슬롯 1레벨당 피해가 1d8점씩 증가합니다.
🎲 3d8 = 13

**라비니아:** Primal Savagery
You channel primal magic to cause your teeth or fingernails to sharpen, ready
to deliver a corrosive attack. Make a melee spell attack against one creature
within 5 feet of you. On a hit, the target takes 1d10 acid damage. After you
make the attack, your teeth or fingernails return to normal.
The spell’s damage increases by 1d10 when you reach 5th level (2d10), 11th
level (3d10), and 17th level (4d10).
🎲 1d20 + 5 + 3 = 26
🎲 2d10 = 15

**럭키:** "참나. 변절했으면서 프로정신이라니."

**라비니아:** Wrath of the Sea
As a Bonus Action, you can expend a use of your Wild Shape to manifest a 5-
foot Emanation that takes the form of ocean spray that surrounds you for 10
minutes. It ends early if you dismiss it (no action required), manifest it again, or
have the Incapacitated condition.
When you manifest the Emanation and as a Bonus Action on your subsequent
turns, you can choose another creature you can see in the Emanation. The
target must succeed on a Constitution saving throw against your spell save DC
or take Cold damage and, if the creature is Large or smaller, be pushed up to 15
feet away from you. To determine this damage, roll a number of d6s equal to
your Wisdom modifier (minimum of one die).

**라비니아:** Startling Speed
Your movements are so swift that you are almost invisible when in motion. If
you move at least 10 feet on your turn, attack rolls against you have
disadvantage until the start of your next turn. This feature does not function if
you are incapacitated or restrained. You can use this ability a number of rounds
per day equal to your level.

A bright streak flashes from you to a point you choose within range and then
blossoms with a low roar into a fiery explosion. Each creature in a 20-foot-

8d6 Fire damage on a failed save or half as much damage on a successful one.
Flammable objects in the area that aren’t being worn or carried start burning.
Using a Higher-Level Spell Slot. The damage increases by 1d6 for each spell
slot level above 3.

**Fade Away:** You have learned to avoid notice at all costs, letting you momentarily obscure
yourself from observation. As a Bonus Action, you can take the Hide action to
conceal yourself without needing to be Heavily Obscured or behind Three-
Quarters Cover or Total Cover. You need not be out of a creature’s line of sight
to use this ability.
You become visible at the start of your next turn unless you have moved into a
position that allows you to use the Hide action normally. You can use this
feature a number of times equal to your Proficiency Bonus, regaining all
expended uses when you finish a Long Rest.

**럭키:** Monk's Focus: Flurry of Blows
Your focus and martial training allow you to harness a well of extraordinary
energy within yourself. This energy is represented by Focus Points. Your Monk
level determines the number of points you have, as shown in the Focus Points
column of the Monk Features table.
You can expend these points to enhance or fuel certain Monk features. You start
knowing three such features: Flurry of Blows, Patient Defense, and Step of the
Wind, each of which is detailed below.
When you expend a Focus Point, it is unavailable until you finish a Short or
Long Rest, at the end of which you regain all your expended points.
Some features that use Focus Points require your target to make a saving throw.
The save DC equals 8 plus your Wisdom modifier and Proficiency Bonus.
Flurry of Blows. You can expend 1 Focus Point to make two Unarmed Strikes as
a Bonus Action.
Patient Defense. You can take the Disengage action as a Bonus Action.
Alternatively, you can expend 1 Focus Point to take both the Disengage and the
Dodge actions as a Bonus Action.
Step of the Wind. You can take the Dash action as a Bonus Action. Alternatively,
you can expend 1 Focus Point to take both the Disengage and Dash actions as a
Bonus Action, and your jump distance is doubled for the turn.

**Gamemaster:** 요안의 근위병 takes 11 damage

**HP 업데이트 됨 두 배 적용 취소:** x1
58-11(11)=47

**럭키:** Unarmed Strike
Instead of using a weapon to make a melee attack, you can use a punch, kick,
head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a
melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a
target within 5 feet of you.
Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for
its effect.
Damage. You make an attack roll against the target. Your bonus to the roll
equals your Strength modifier plus your Proficiency Bonus. On a hit, the target
takes Bludgeoning damage equal to 1 plus your Strength modifier.
Grapple. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or it has the Grappled condition. The DC for the saving throw
and any escape attempts equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency
Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger
than you and if you have a hand free to grab it.
Shove. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone
condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and
Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one
size larger than you.
🎲 2d20kh + 5 + 3 + 1 = 15
🎲 1d8 + 5 + 1 = 11

**럭키:** Open Hand Technique
Whenever you hit a creature with an attack granted by your Flurry of Blows, you
can impose one of the following effects on that target.
Addle. The target can’t make Opportunity Attacks until the start of its next turn.
Push. The target must succeed on a Strength saving throw or be pushed up to
15 feet away from you.
Topple. The target must succeed on a Dexterity saving throw or have the Prone
condition.

**피에스타:** Blood Bolt
You hurl a twisting bolt of blood at a creature within range. Make a ranged spell
attack against the target. On a hit, the target takes 1d6 Necrotic damage, and
you gain a number of Temporary Hit Points equal to your Proficiency Bonus.
Cantrip Upgrade. The damage increases by 1d6 when you reach levels 5 (2d6),
11 (3d6), and 17 (4d6).
🎲 1d20 + 5 + 2 = 18
🎲 2d6 = 3

This spell accelerates or decelerates an attack (see the chosen effect below) the
instant before it strikes, lessening or multiplying its force.
Accelerate. The target takes an extra 2d6 damage from the attack. This extra
damage is the same type dealt by the triggering attack.
Decelerate. Reduce the damage the target takes by 2d6 (to a minimum of 0
damage).

increases by 1d6 for each slot level above 1.

**Deflect Attacks:** When an attack roll hits you and its damage includes Bludgeoning, Piercing, or
Slashing damage, you can take a Reaction to reduce the attack’s total damage
against you. The reduction equals 1d10 plus your Dexterity modifier and Monk
level.
If you reduce the damage to 0, you can expend 1 Focus Point to redirect some
of the attack’s force. If you do so, choose a creature you can see within 5 feet of
yourself if the attack was a melee attack or a creature you can see within 60 feet
of yourself that isn’t behind Total Cover if the attack was a ranged attack. That
creature must succeed on a Dexterity saving throw or take damage equal to two
rolls of your Martial Arts die plus your Dexterity modifier. The damage is the
same type dealt by the attack.

**럭키의 턴:** Monk's Focus: Flurry of Blows
Your focus and martial training allow you to harness a well of extraordinary
energy within yourself. This energy is represented by Focus Points. Your Monk
level determines the number of points you have, as shown in the Focus Points
column of the Monk Features table.
You can expend these points to enhance or fuel certain Monk features. You start
knowing three such features: Flurry of Blows, Patient Defense, and Step of the
Wind, each of which is detailed below.
When you expend a Focus Point, it is unavailable until you finish a Short or
Long Rest, at the end of which you regain all your expended points.
Some features that use Focus Points require your target to make a saving throw.
The save DC equals 8 plus your Wisdom modifier and Proficiency Bonus.
Flurry of Blows. You can expend 1 Focus Point to make two Unarmed Strikes as
a Bonus Action.
Patient Defense. You can take the Disengage action as a Bonus Action.
Alternatively, you can expend 1 Focus Point to take both the Disengage and the
Dodge actions as a Bonus Action.
Step of the Wind. You can take the Dash action as a Bonus Action. Alternatively,
you can expend 1 Focus Point to take both the Disengage and Dash actions as a
Bonus Action, and your jump distance is doubled for the turn.

**Gamemaster:** 전령 takes 8 damage

**HP 업데이트 됨 두 배 적용 취소:** x1
112-8(8)=104

**럭키:** Unarmed Strike
Instead of using a weapon to make a melee attack, you can use a punch, kick,
head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a
melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a
target within 5 feet of you.
Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for
its effect.
Damage. You make an attack roll against the target. Your bonus to the roll
equals your Strength modifier plus your Proficiency Bonus. On a hit, the target
takes Bludgeoning damage equal to 1 plus your Strength modifier.
Grapple. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or it has the Grappled condition. The DC for the saving throw
and any escape attempts equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency
Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger
than you and if you have a hand free to grab it.
Shove. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone
condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and
Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one
size larger than you.
🎲 1d20 + 5 + 3 + 1 = 20
🎲 1d8 + 5 + 1 = 8

chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone

**럭키:** Stunning Strike
Once per turn when you hit a creature with a Monk weapon or an Unarmed
Strike, you can expend 1 Focus Point to attempt a stunning strike. The target
must make a Constitution saving throw. On a failed save, the target has the
Stunned condition until the start of your next turn. On a successful save, the
target’s Speed is halved until the start of your next turn, and the next attack roll
made against the target before then has Advantage.

**전령:** "으윽…"
민첩 내성 굴림25 🎲 1d20 + 2 + 3 + 0 = 25

**럭키:** Open Hand Technique
Whenever you hit a creature with an attack granted by your Flurry of Blows, you
can impose one of the following effects on that target.
Addle. The target can’t make Opportunity Attacks until the start of its next turn.
Push. The target must succeed on a Strength saving throw or be pushed up to
15 feet away from you.
Topple. The target must succeed on a Dexterity saving throw or have the Prone
condition.

**요안의 마법병:** Lightning Bolt
A stroke of lightning forming a 100-foot-long, 5-foot-wide Line blasts out from
you in a direction you choose. Each creature in the Line makes a Dexterity
saving throw, taking 8d6 Lightning damage on a failed save or half as much
damage on a successful one.

**럭키:** Unarmed Strike
Instead of using a weapon to make a melee attack, you can use a punch, kick,
head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a
melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a
target within 5 feet of you.
Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for
its effect.
Damage. You make an attack roll against the target. Your bonus to the roll
equals your Strength modifier plus your Proficiency Bonus. On a hit, the target
takes Bludgeoning damage equal to 1 plus your Strength modifier.
Grapple. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or it has the Grappled condition. The DC for the saving throw
and any escape attempts equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency
Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger
than you and if you have a hand free to grab it.
Shove. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone
condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and
Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one
size larger than you.

Grazing Shot [Maneuver]
When you miss with a ranged attack roll, you can expend one Risk Die (no
action required) to deal damage to that creature equal to a roll of the die plus
your Dexterity modifier (minimum of 1). This damage is the same type dealt by
the weapon, and the damage can be increased only by increasing the ability
modifier. You can only deal this damage once per turn.
🎲 1d8 + 5 = 6

**Rage:** You can imbue yourself with a primal power called Rage, a force that grants you
extraordinary might and resilience. You can enter it as a Bonus Action if you
aren't wearing Heavy armor.
You can enter your Rage the number of times shown for your Barbarian level in
the Rages column of the Barbarian Features table (currently
@scale.barbarian.rages). You regain one expended use when you finish a Short
Rest, and you regain all expended uses when you finish a Long Rest.
While active, your Rage follows the rules below.
Damage Resistance. You have Resistance to Bludgeoning, Piercing, and
Slashing damage.
Rage Damage. When you make an attack using Strength—with either a weapon
or an Unarmed Strike—and deal damage to the target, you gain a bonus to the
damage that increases as you gain levels as a Barbarian, as shown in the Rage
Damage column of the Barbarian Features table.
Strength Advantage. You have Advantage on Strength checks and Strength
saving throws.
No Concentration or Spells. You can't maintain Concentration, and you can't
cast spells.
Duration. The Rage lasts until the end of your next turn, and it ends early if you
don Heavy armor or have the Incapacitated condition. If your Rage is still active
on your next turn, you can extend the Rage for another round by doing one of
the following:
Make an attack roll against an enemy.
Force an enemy to make a saving throw.
Take a Bonus Action to extend your Rage.
Each time the Rage is extended, it lasts until the end of your next turn. You can
maintain a Rage for up to 10 minutes.

An event in your past left an indelible mark on you, infusing you with simmering
magic. As a Bonus Action, you can unleash that magic for 1 minute, during
which you gain the following benefits:
The spell save DC of your Sorcerer spells increases by 1.
You have Advantage on the attack rolls of Sorcerer spells you cast.
You can use this feature twice, and you regain all expended uses of it when you
finish a Long Rest.

**요안:** Shield
An imperceptible barrier of magical force protects you. Until the start of your
next turn, you have a +5 bonus to AC, including against the triggering attack,
and you take no damage from Magic Missile.

**피에스타:** Blood Bolt
You hurl a twisting bolt of blood at a creature within range. Make a ranged spell
attack against the target. On a hit, the target takes 1d6 Necrotic damage, and
you gain a number of Temporary Hit Points equal to your Proficiency Bonus.
Cantrip Upgrade. The damage increases by 1d6 when you reach levels 5 (2d6),
11 (3d6), and 17 (4d6).

Monk's Focus: Flurry of Blows
Your focus and martial training allow you to harness a well of extraordinary
energy within yourself. This energy is represented by Focus Points. Your Monk
level determines the number of points you have, as shown in the Focus Points
column of the Monk Features table.
You can expend these points to enhance or fuel certain Monk features. You start
knowing three such features: Flurry of Blows, Patient Defense, and Step of the
Wind, each of which is detailed below.
When you expend a Focus Point, it is unavailable until you finish a Short or
Long Rest, at the end of which you regain all your expended points.
Some features that use Focus Points require your target to make a saving throw.
The save DC equals 8 plus your Wisdom modifier and Proficiency Bonus.
Flurry of Blows. You can expend 1 Focus Point to make two Unarmed Strikes as
a Bonus Action.
Patient Defense. You can take the Disengage action as a Bonus Action.
Alternatively, you can expend 1 Focus Point to take both the Disengage and the
Dodge actions as a Bonus Action.
Step of the Wind. You can take the Dash action as a Bonus Action. Alternatively,
you can expend 1 Focus Point to take both the Disengage and Dash actions as a
Bonus Action, and your jump distance is doubled for the turn.
"오아시스 템플 제 5 타격술! 상어의 사냥!"

**Gamemaster:** 요안 takes 14 damage

**HP 업데이트 됨 두 배 적용 취소:** x1
120-14(14)=106

**럭키:** Unarmed Strike
Instead of using a weapon to make a melee attack, you can use a punch, kick,
head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a
melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a
target within 5 feet of you.
Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for
its effect.
Damage. You make an attack roll against the target. Your bonus to the roll
equals your Strength modifier plus your Proficiency Bonus. On a hit, the target
takes Bludgeoning damage equal to 1 plus your Strength modifier.
Grapple. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or it has the Grappled condition. The DC for the saving throw
and any escape attempts equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency
Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger
than you and if you have a hand free to grab it.
Shove. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone
condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and
Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one
size larger than you.
🎲 1d20 + 5 + 3 + 1 = 21
🎲 1d8 + 5 + 1 = 14

**Unarmed Strike:** Instead of using a weapon to make a melee attack, you can use a punch, kick,
head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a
melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a
target within 5 feet of you.
Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for
its effect.
Damage. You make an attack roll against the target. Your bonus to the roll
equals your Strength modifier plus your Proficiency Bonus. On a hit, the target
takes Bludgeoning damage equal to 1 plus your Strength modifier.
Grapple. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or it has the Grappled condition. The DC for the saving throw
and any escape attempts equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency
Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger
than you and if you have a hand free to grab it.
Shove. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone
condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and
Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one
size larger than you.

**럭키:** Unarmed Strike
Instead of using a weapon to make a melee attack, you can use a punch, kick,
head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a
melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a
target within 5 feet of you.
Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for
its effect.
Damage. You make an attack roll against the target. Your bonus to the roll
equals your Strength modifier plus your Proficiency Bonus. On a hit, the target
takes Bludgeoning damage equal to 1 plus your Strength modifier.
Grapple. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or it has the Grappled condition. The DC for the saving throw
and any escape attempts equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency
Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger
than you and if you have a hand free to grab it.
Shove. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone
condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and
Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one
size larger than you.

**요안:** "이런..!"
건강 내성 굴림17 🎲 1d20 + 2 = 17

**럭키:** Stunning Strike
Once per turn when you hit a creature with a Monk weapon or an Unarmed
Strike, you can expend 1 Focus Point to attempt a stunning strike. The target
must make a Constitution saving throw. On a failed save, the target has the
Stunned condition until the start of your next turn. On a successful save, the
target’s Speed is halved until the start of your next turn, and the next attack roll
made against the target before then has Advantage.

**요안:** 민첩 내성 굴림14 🎲 1d20 + 2 + 0 = 14

**럭키:** Open Hand Technique
Whenever you hit a creature with an attack granted by your Flurry of Blows, you
can impose one of the following effects on that target.
Addle. The target can’t make Opportunity Attacks until the start of its next turn.
Push. The target must succeed on a Strength saving throw or be pushed up to
15 feet away from you.
Topple. The target must succeed on a Dexterity saving throw or have the Prone
condition.

melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a
target within 5 feet of you.
Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for
its effect.
Damage. You make an attack roll against the target. Your bonus to the roll

takes Bludgeoning damage equal to 1 plus your Strength modifier.

**Crimson Lash:** As part of casting this spell, you must expend one Hit Point Die or the spell
automatically fails. A writhing lash of coagulated blood springs from your hand
with the following properties:
It counts as a Simple weapon with which you are proficient.
It has the Light, Finesse, and Reach properties.
You can use your spellcasting ability modifier instead of your Strength or
Dexterity modifier for the attack and damage rolls with this weapon.
Its damage die is the same as the Hit Point Die expended to cast the spell,
and the damage dealt is Necrotic.
Each time a creature takes damage from this weapon, its Hit Point
maximum decreases by an amount equal to the damage taken.
Using a Higher-Level Spell Slot. If you cast this spell using a level 3-4 spell
slot, you can make two weapon attacks with this weapon when you take the
Attack action. If you use a level 5+ spell slot, you can make three weapon
attacks with this weapon when you take the Attack action.

Eldritch Claw Tattoo
Produced by a special needle, this magic tattoo depicts clawlike forms and
other jagged shapes.
Tattoo Attunement. To attune to this item, you hold the needle to your skin
where you want the tattoo to appear, pressing the needle there throughout the
attunement process. When the attunement is complete, the needle turns into
the ink that becomes the tattoo, which appears on the skin.
If your attunement to the tattoo ends, the tattoo vanishes, and the needle
reappears in your space.
Magical Strikes. While the tattoo is on your skin, your unarmed strikes are
considered magical for the purpose of overcoming immunity and resistance to
nonmagical attacks, and you gain a +1 bonus to attack and damage rolls with
unarmed strikes.
Eldritch Maul. As a bonus action, you can empower the tattoo for 1 minute. For
the duration, each of your melee attacks with a weapon or an unarmed strike
can reach a target up to 15 feet away from you, as inky tendrils launch toward
the target. In addition, your melee attacks deal an extra 3 (1d6) 역장 damage on
a hit. Once used, this bonus action can’t be used again until the next dawn.

**Finger Guns:** You extend your forefinger and thumb, a dangerous gesture mimicking a gun.
For the duration, your hand counts as a Simple Ranged weapon with a range of
60/240 feet and the Slow mastery property. You can use your spellcasting ability
instead of Dexterity for the attack rolls of this weapon. On a hit, the weapon
deals 2d6 Force damage and doesn’t add your ability modifier to damage.
Cantrip Upgrade. The weapon’s normal range increases by 30 feet and its long
range increases by 120 feet when you reach levels 5 (90/360 feet), 11 (120/480
feet), and 17 (150/600 feet).

**라비니아:** Spike Growth
The ground in a 20-foot-radius Sphere centered on a point within range sprouts
hard spikes and thorns. The area becomes Difficult Terrain for the duration.
When a creature moves into or within the area, it takes 2d4 Piercing damage for
every 5 feet it travels.
The transformation of the ground is camouflaged to look natural. Any creature
that can’t see the area when the spell is cast must take a Search action and
succeed on a Wisdom (Perception or Survival) check against your spell save DC
to recognize the terrain as hazardous before entering it.

**Wrath of the Sea:** As a Bonus Action, you can expend a use of your Wild Shape to manifest a 5-
foot Emanation that takes the form of ocean spray that surrounds you for 10
minutes. It ends early if you dismiss it (no action required), manifest it again, or
have the Incapacitated condition.
When you manifest the Emanation and as a Bonus Action on your subsequent
turns, you can choose another creature you can see in the Emanation. The
target must succeed on a Constitution saving throw against your spell save DC
or take Cold damage and, if the creature is Large or smaller, be pushed up to 15
feet away from you. To determine this damage, roll a number of d6s equal to
your Wisdom modifier (minimum of one die).

This spell accelerates or decelerates an attack (see the chosen effect below) the

damage is the same type dealt by the triggering attack.

damage).
Using a Higher-Level Spell Slot. The extra damage or reduction in damage
increases by 1d6 for each slot level above 1.

**Unarmed Strike:** Instead of using a weapon to make a melee attack, you can use a punch, kick,
head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a
melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a
target within 5 feet of you.
Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for
its effect.
Damage. You make an attack roll against the target. Your bonus to the roll
equals your Strength modifier plus your Proficiency Bonus. On a hit, the target
takes Bludgeoning damage equal to 1 plus your Strength modifier.
Grapple. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or it has the Grappled condition. The DC for the saving throw
and any escape attempts equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency
Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger
than you and if you have a hand free to grab it.
Shove. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone
condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and
Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one
size larger than you.

**럭키:** Unarmed Strike
Instead of using a weapon to make a melee attack, you can use a punch, kick,
head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a
melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a
target within 5 feet of you.
Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for
its effect.
Damage. You make an attack roll against the target. Your bonus to the roll
equals your Strength modifier plus your Proficiency Bonus. On a hit, the target
takes Bludgeoning damage equal to 1 plus your Strength modifier.
Grapple. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or it has the Grappled condition. The DC for the saving throw
and any escape attempts equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency
Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger
than you and if you have a hand free to grab it.
Shove. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone
condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and
Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one
size larger than you.

난 다시 간다!
Monk's Focus: Flurry of Blows
Your focus and martial training allow you to harness a well of extraordinary
energy within yourself. This energy is represented by Focus Points. Your Monk
level determines the number of points you have, as shown in the Focus Points
column of the Monk Features table.
You can expend these points to enhance or fuel certain Monk features. You start
knowing three such features: Flurry of Blows, Patient Defense, and Step of the
Wind, each of which is detailed below.
When you expend a Focus Point, it is unavailable until you finish a Short or
Long Rest, at the end of which you regain all your expended points.
Some features that use Focus Points require your target to make a saving throw.
The save DC equals 8 plus your Wisdom modifier and Proficiency Bonus.
Flurry of Blows. You can expend 1 Focus Point to make two Unarmed Strikes as
a Bonus Action.
Patient Defense. You can take the Disengage action as a Bonus Action.
Alternatively, you can expend 1 Focus Point to take both the Disengage and the
Dodge actions as a Bonus Action.
Step of the Wind. You can take the Dash action as a Bonus Action. Alternatively,
you can expend 1 Focus Point to take both the Disengage and Dash actions as a
Bonus Action, and your jump distance is doubled for the turn.

head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a

chooses which), or it has the Grappled condition. The DC for the saving throw
and any escape attempts equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency
Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger

**요안의 호위병:** 근력 내성 굴림21 🎲 1d20 + 8 + 3 = 21

**럭키:** Unarmed Strike
Instead of using a weapon to make a melee attack, you can use a punch, kick,
head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a
melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a
target within 5 feet of you.
Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for
its effect.
Damage. You make an attack roll against the target. Your bonus to the roll
equals your Strength modifier plus your Proficiency Bonus. On a hit, the target
takes Bludgeoning damage equal to 1 plus your Strength modifier.
Grapple. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or it has the Grappled condition. The DC for the saving throw
and any escape attempts equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency
Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger
than you and if you have a hand free to grab it.
Shove. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone
condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and
Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one
size larger than you.

**요안의 호위병:** 민첩 내성 굴림2 🎲 1d20 + 0 + 0 = 2

**럭키:** Open Hand Technique
Whenever you hit a creature with an attack granted by your Flurry of Blows, you
can impose one of the following effects on that target.
Addle. The target can’t make Opportunity Attacks until the start of its next turn.
Push. The target must succeed on a Strength saving throw or be pushed up to
15 feet away from you.
Topple. The target must succeed on a Dexterity saving throw or have the Prone
condition.

**Fade Away:** You have learned to avoid notice at all costs, letting you momentarily obscure
yourself from observation. As a Bonus Action, you can take the Hide action to
conceal yourself without needing to be Heavily Obscured or behind Three-
Quarters Cover or Total Cover. You need not be out of a creature’s line of sight
to use this ability.
You become visible at the start of your next turn unless you have moved into a
position that allows you to use the Hide action normally. You can use this
feature a number of times equal to your Proficiency Bonus, regaining all
expended uses when you finish a Long Rest.

You can throw aside all concern for defense to attack with increased ferocity.

**럭키:** Deflect Attacks
When an attack roll hits you and its damage includes Bludgeoning, Piercing, or
Slashing damage, you can take a Reaction to reduce the attack’s total damage
against you. The reduction equals 1d10 plus your Dexterity modifier and Monk
level.
If you reduce the damage to 0, you can expend 1 Focus Point to redirect some
of the attack’s force. If you do so, choose a creature you can see within 5 feet of
yourself if the attack was a melee attack or a creature you can see within 60 feet
of yourself that isn’t behind Total Cover if the attack was a ranged attack. That
creature must succeed on a Dexterity saving throw or take damage equal to two
rolls of your Martial Arts die plus your Dexterity modifier. The damage is the
same type dealt by the attack.
🎲 1d10 + 5 + 5 = 12

칼날의 방아쇠를 당길 수 있습니다. 공압 찌르기를 하면 무기 윗부분이 앞으로 호를 그리며

병원균이 마법에 의해 다시 활성화되어 추가로 1d8 독 피해를 입힙니다.

Accelerate. The target takes an extra 2d6 damage from the attack. This extra

Decelerate. Reduce the damage the target takes by 2d6 (to a minimum of 0
damage).
Using a Higher-Level Spell Slot. The extra damage or reduction in damage
increases by 1d6 for each slot level above 1.
🎲 6d6 + 2d8 + 2d6 = 52

Grazing Shot [Maneuver]
When you miss with a ranged attack roll, you can expend one Risk Die (no
action required) to deal damage to that creature equal to a roll of the die plus
your Dexterity modifier (minimum of 1). This damage is the same type dealt by
the weapon, and the damage can be increased only by increasing the ability
modifier. You can only deal this damage once per turn.
🎲 1d8 + 5 = 11

attack against the target. On a hit, the target takes 1d6 Necrotic damage, and
you gain a number of Temporary Hit Points equal to your Proficiency Bonus.
Cantrip Upgrade. The damage increases by 1d6 when you reach levels 5 (2d6),
11 (3d6), and 17 (4d6).

**아르시안 엘다인:** Fireball
A bright streak flashes from you to a point you choose within range and then
blossoms with a low roar into a fiery explosion. Each creature in a 20-foot-
radius Sphere centered on that point makes a Dexterity saving throw, taking
8d6 Fire damage on a failed save or half as much damage on a successful one.
Flammable objects in the area that aren’t being worn or carried start burning.
Using a Higher-Level Spell Slot. The damage increases by 1d6 for each spell
slot level above 3.
🎲 8d6 = 27

**럭키:** Unarmed Strike (공격)
Instead of using a weapon to make a melee attack, you can use a punch, kick,
head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a
melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a
target within 5 feet of you.
Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for
its effect.
Damage. You make an attack roll against the target. Your bonus to the roll
equals your Strength modifier plus your Proficiency Bonus. On a hit, the target
takes Bludgeoning damage equal to 1 plus your Strength modifier.
Grapple. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or it has the Grappled condition. The DC for the saving throw
and any escape attempts equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency
Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger
than you and if you have a hand free to grab it.
Shove. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone
condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and
Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one
size larger than you.
🎲 1d20 + 5 + 3 + 1 = 14

**인스피레이션 리롤:** Instead of using a weapon to make a melee attack, you can use a punch, kick,
head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a
melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a
target within 5 feet of you.
Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for
its effect.
Damage. You make an attack roll against the target. Your bonus to the roll
equals your Strength modifier plus your Proficiency Bonus. On a hit, the target
takes Bludgeoning damage equal to 1 plus your Strength modifier.
Grapple. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or it has the Grappled condition. The DC for the saving throw
and any escape attempts equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency
Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger
than you and if you have a hand free to grab it.
Shove. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone
condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and
Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one
size larger than you.
🎲 1d20 + 5 + 3 + 1 = 20

**럭키:** 인스피레이션 리롤
Instead of using a weapon to make a melee attack, you can use a punch, kick,
head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a
melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a
target within 5 feet of you.
Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for
its effect.
Damage. You make an attack roll against the target. Your bonus to the roll
equals your Strength modifier plus your Proficiency Bonus. On a hit, the target
takes Bludgeoning damage equal to 1 plus your Strength modifier.
Grapple. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or it has the Grappled condition. The DC for the saving throw
and any escape attempts equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency
Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger
than you and if you have a hand free to grab it.
Shove. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone
condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and
Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one
size larger than you.
🎲 1d20 + 999 + 5 + 3 + 1 = 1028
🎲 1d8 + 5 + 1 = 10

head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a

target within 5 feet of you.
Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for
its effect.
Damage. You make an attack roll against the target. Your bonus to the roll
equals your Strength modifier plus your Proficiency Bonus. On a hit, the target
takes Bludgeoning damage equal to 1 plus your Strength modifier.
Grapple. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or it has the Grappled condition. The DC for the saving throw
and any escape attempts equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency
Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger
than you and if you have a hand free to grab it.
Shove. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone
condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and
Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one
size larger than you.

**럭키:** Deflect Attacks
When an attack roll hits you and its damage includes Bludgeoning, Piercing, or
Slashing damage, you can take a Reaction to reduce the attack’s total damage
against you. The reduction equals 1d10 plus your Dexterity modifier and Monk
level.
If you reduce the damage to 0, you can expend 1 Focus Point to redirect some
of the attack’s force. If you do so, choose a creature you can see within 5 feet of
yourself if the attack was a melee attack or a creature you can see within 60 feet
of yourself that isn’t behind Total Cover if the attack was a ranged attack. That
creature must succeed on a Dexterity saving throw or take damage equal to two
rolls of your Martial Arts die plus your Dexterity modifier. The damage is the
same type dealt by the attack.

**🎲 1d10 + 5 + 5 =:** 럭키 takes 1 damage

Accelerate/Decelerate
This spell accelerates or decelerates an attack (see the chosen effect below) the
instant before it strikes, lessening or multiplying its force.
Accelerate. The target takes an extra 2d6 damage from the attack. This extra
damage is the same type dealt by the triggering attack.
Decelerate. Reduce the damage the target takes by 2d6 (to a minimum of 0
damage).
Using a Higher-Level Spell Slot. The extra damage or reduction in damage
increases by 1d6 for each slot level above 1.

때마다 특별한 명령이나 경고를 발할 수 있습니다. 해당 생물은 친위대 대장의 말을 듣고 이
해할 수 있다면 굴림에 d4 를 더할 수 있습니다. 생물은 한 번에 하나의 리더십 주사위만 사
용할 수 있습니다. 산적 두목이 무력화 되면 이 효과는 사라집니다.

**라비니아:** Wrath of the Sea
As a Bonus Action, you can expend a use of your Wild Shape to manifest a 5-
foot Emanation that takes the form of ocean spray that surrounds you for 10
minutes. It ends early if you dismiss it (no action required), manifest it again, or
have the Incapacitated condition.
When you manifest the Emanation and as a Bonus Action on your subsequent
turns, you can choose another creature you can see in the Emanation. The
target must succeed on a Constitution saving throw against your spell save DC
or take Cold damage and, if the creature is Large or smaller, be pushed up to 15
feet away from you. To determine this damage, roll a number of d6s equal to
your Wisdom modifier (minimum of one die).

you move at least 10 feet on your turn, attack rolls against you have
disadvantage until the start of your next turn. This feature does not function if
you are incapacitated or restrained. You can use this ability a number of rounds
per day equal to your level.

**Darkness:** For the duration, magical Darkness spreads from a point within range and fills a
15-foot-radius Sphere. Darkvision can’t see through it, and nonmagical light
can’t illuminate it.
Alternatively, you cast the spell on an object that isn’t being worn or carried,
causing the Darkness to fill a 15-foot Emanation originating from that object.
Covering that object with something opaque, such as a bowl or helm, blocks
the Darkness.
If any of this spell’s area overlaps with an area of Bright Light or Dim Light
created by a spell of level 2 or lower, that other spell is dispelled.

**럭키:** Deflect Attacks
When an attack roll hits you and its damage includes Bludgeoning, Piercing, or
Slashing damage, you can take a Reaction to reduce the attack’s total damage
against you. The reduction equals 1d10 plus your Dexterity modifier and Monk
level.
If you reduce the damage to 0, you can expend 1 Focus Point to redirect some
of the attack’s force. If you do so, choose a creature you can see within 5 feet of
yourself if the attack was a melee attack or a creature you can see within 60 feet
of yourself that isn’t behind Total Cover if the attack was a ranged attack. That
creature must succeed on a Dexterity saving throw or take damage equal to two
rolls of your Martial Arts die plus your Dexterity modifier. The damage is the
same type dealt by the attack.

**🎲 1d10 + 5 + 5 =:** 럭키 takes 8 damage

**럭키:** Monk's Focus: Flurry of Blows
Your focus and martial training allow you to harness a well of extraordinary
energy within yourself. This energy is represented by Focus Points. Your Monk
level determines the number of points you have, as shown in the Focus Points
column of the Monk Features table.
You can expend these points to enhance or fuel certain Monk features. You start
knowing three such features: Flurry of Blows, Patient Defense, and Step of the
Wind, each of which is detailed below.
When you expend a Focus Point, it is unavailable until you finish a Short or
Long Rest, at the end of which you regain all your expended points.
Some features that use Focus Points require your target to make a saving throw.
The save DC equals 8 plus your Wisdom modifier and Proficiency Bonus.
Flurry of Blows. You can expend 1 Focus Point to make two Unarmed Strikes as
a Bonus Action.
Patient Defense. You can take the Disengage action as a Bonus Action.
Alternatively, you can expend 1 Focus Point to take both the Disengage and the
Dodge actions as a Bonus Action.
Step of the Wind. You can take the Dash action as a Bonus Action. Alternatively,
you can expend 1 Focus Point to take both the Disengage and Dash actions as a
Bonus Action, and your jump distance is doubled for the turn.

**라비니아:** ….

**럭키:** Unarmed Strike
Instead of using a weapon to make a melee attack, you can use a punch, kick,
head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a
melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a
target within 5 feet of you.
Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for
its effect.
Damage. You make an attack roll against the target. Your bonus to the roll
equals your Strength modifier plus your Proficiency Bonus. On a hit, the target
takes Bludgeoning damage equal to 1 plus your Strength modifier.
Grapple. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or it has the Grappled condition. The DC for the saving throw
and any escape attempts equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency
Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger
than you and if you have a hand free to grab it.
Shove. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone
condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and
Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one
size larger than you.
🎲 1d20 + 5 + 3 + 1 = 13

**럭키:** Open Hand Technique
Whenever you hit a creature with an attack granted by your Flurry of Blows, you
can impose one of the following effects on that target.
Addle. The target can’t make Opportunity Attacks until the start of its next turn.
Push. The target must succeed on a Strength saving throw or be pushed up to
15 feet away from you.
Topple. The target must succeed on a Dexterity saving throw or have the Prone
condition.

**럭키:** Stunning Strike
Once per turn when you hit a creature with a Monk weapon or an Unarmed
Strike, you can expend 1 Focus Point to attempt a stunning strike. The target
must make a Constitution saving throw. On a failed save, the target has the
Stunned condition until the start of your next turn. On a successful save, the
target’s Speed is halved until the start of your next turn, and the next attack roll
made against the target before then has Advantage.

**Unarmed Strike:** Instead of using a weapon to make a melee attack, you can use a punch, kick,
head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a
melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a
target within 5 feet of you.
Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for
its effect.

equals your Strength modifier plus your Proficiency Bonus. On a hit, the target
takes Bludgeoning damage equal to 1 plus your Strength modifier.
Grapple. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or it has the Grappled condition. The DC for the saving throw
and any escape attempts equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency
Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger
than you and if you have a hand free to grab it.
Shove. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone
condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and
Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one
size larger than you.

**요안의 근위병:** Parry
The bandit lord adds 2 to its AC against one melee attack that would hit it. To
do so, the bandit lord must see the attacker and be wielding a weapon.

**Gamemaster:** HP 업데이트 됨 두 배 적용 취소

**x:** 64-11(11)=53

**라비니아:** Primal Savagery
You channel primal magic to cause your teeth or fingernails to sharpen, ready
to deliver a corrosive attack. Make a melee spell attack against one creature
within 5 feet of you. On a hit, the target takes 1d10 acid damage. After you
make the attack, your teeth or fingernails return to normal.
The spell’s damage increases by 1d10 when you reach 5th level (2d10), 11th

**밀메:** Rime's Binding Ice
A burst of cold energy emanates from you in a 30-foot cone. Each creature in
that area must make a Constitution saving throw. On a failed save, a creature
takes 3d8 cold damage and is hindered by ice formations for 1 minute, or until
it or another creature within reach of it uses an action to break away the ice. A
creature hindered by ice has its speed reduced to 0. On a successful save, a
creature takes half as much damage and isn’t hindered by ice.
At Higher Levels. When you cast this spell using a spell slot of 3rd level or
higher, increase the cold damage by 1d8 for each slot level above 2nd.

**럭키:** Monk's Focus: Flurry of Blows
Your focus and martial training allow you to harness a well of extraordinary
energy within yourself. This energy is represented by Focus Points. Your Monk
level determines the number of points you have, as shown in the Focus Points
column of the Monk Features table.
You can expend these points to enhance or fuel certain Monk features. You start
knowing three such features: Flurry of Blows, Patient Defense, and Step of the
Wind, each of which is detailed below.
When you expend a Focus Point, it is unavailable until you finish a Short or
Long Rest, at the end of which you regain all your expended points.
Some features that use Focus Points require your target to make a saving throw.
The save DC equals 8 plus your Wisdom modifier and Proficiency Bonus.
Flurry of Blows. You can expend 1 Focus Point to make two Unarmed Strikes as
a Bonus Action.
Patient Defense. You can take the Disengage action as a Bonus Action.
Alternatively, you can expend 1 Focus Point to take both the Disengage and the
Dodge actions as a Bonus Action.
Step of the Wind. You can take the Dash action as a Bonus Action. Alternatively,
you can expend 1 Focus Point to take both the Disengage and Dash actions as a
Bonus Action, and your jump distance is doubled for the turn.

**아르시안 엘다인:** (대부분은 버그입니다

**HP 업데이트 됨 두 배 적용 취소:** x1
30-13(13)=17

**럭키:** Unarmed Strike
Instead of using a weapon to make a melee attack, you can use a punch, kick,
head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a
melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a
target within 5 feet of you.
Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for
its effect.
Damage. You make an attack roll against the target. Your bonus to the roll
equals your Strength modifier plus your Proficiency Bonus. On a hit, the target
takes Bludgeoning damage equal to 1 plus your Strength modifier.
Grapple. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or it has the Grappled condition. The DC for the saving throw
and any escape attempts equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency
Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger
than you and if you have a hand free to grab it.
Shove. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone
condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and
Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one
size larger than you.
🎲 2d20kh + 5 + 3 + 1 = 18
🎲 1d8 + 5 + 1 = 13

**Unarmed Strike:** Instead of using a weapon to make a melee attack, you can use a punch, kick,
head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a
melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a
target within 5 feet of you.
Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for
its effect.
Damage. You make an attack roll against the target. Your bonus to the roll
equals your Strength modifier plus your Proficiency Bonus. On a hit, the target
takes Bludgeoning damage equal to 1 plus your Strength modifier.
Grapple. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or it has the Grappled condition. The DC for the saving throw
and any escape attempts equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency
Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger
than you and if you have a hand free to grab it.
Shove. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone
condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and
Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one
size larger than you.

**럭키:** Stunning Strike
Once per turn when you hit a creature with a Monk weapon or an Unarmed
Strike, you can expend 1 Focus Point to attempt a stunning strike. The target
must make a Constitution saving throw. On a failed save, the target has the
Stunned condition until the start of your next turn. On a successful save, the
target’s Speed is halved until the start of your next turn, and the next attack roll
made against the target before then has Advantage.

**ㄹㅇ이가:** 럭키 gains 1 temp HP

Accelerate/Decelerate
This spell accelerates or decelerates an attack (see the chosen effect below) the
instant before it strikes, lessening or multiplying its force.
Accelerate. The target takes an extra 2d6 damage from the attack. This extra
damage is the same type dealt by the triggering attack.
Decelerate. Reduce the damage the target takes by 2d6 (to a minimum of 0
damage).
Using a Higher-Level Spell Slot. The extra damage or reduction in damage
increases by 1d6 for each slot level above 1.
